function sjcl.bitArray.bitSlice (a, b, c)

  • description and source-code
    bitArray.bitSlice = function (a, b, c){a=sjcl.bitArray.$(a.slice(b/32),32-(b&31)).slice(1);return void 0===c?a:sjcl.bitArray.clamp(a,c-b)}

function sjcl.bitArray.byteswapM (a)

function sjcl.json.decode (a)

  • description and source-code
